    FROM [AspNetUsers] AS [a]
    WHERE [a].[UserType] IN (N'UserBaseModel', N'ClubAdministrator', N'ClubManager', N'DivisionManager', N'Fan', N'Officials', N'Player', N'SportsMember', N'SystemAdministrator')
) AS [a0] ON [t].[CreatedById] = [a0].[Id]
INNER JOIN (
    SELECT [a1].[Id], [a1].[AccessFailedCount], [a1].[ConcurrencyStamp], [a1].[Email], [a1].[EmailConfirmed], [a1].[LockoutEnabled], [a1].[LockoutEnd], [a1].[NormalizedEmail], [a1].[NormalizedUserName], [a1].[PasswordHash], [a1].[PhoneNumber], [a1].[PhoneNumberConfirmed], [a1].[SecurityStamp], [a1].[TwoFactorEnabled], [a1].[UserName], [a1].[UserType], [a1].[CreatedBy], [a1].[CreatedDateTime], [a1].[DateOfBirth], [a1].[FirstName], [a1].[IsActive], [a1].[IsDeleted], [a1].[IsFirstTimeLogin], [a1].[IsSuspended], [a1].[LastName], [a1].[ModifiedBy], [a1].[ModifiedDateTime], [a1].[ProfilePicture], [a1].[ClubId], [a1].[DivisionId], [a1].[ClubManager_ClubId], [a1].[ClubManager_DivisionId], [a1].[IsContractEnded], [a1].[DivisionManager_DivisionId], [a1].[Officials_DivisionId], [a1].[Player_ClubId], [a1].[Player_DivisionId], [a1].[EndDate], [a1].[HasPlayed], [a1].[IsContractSigned], [a1].[IsOnPitch], [a1].[JerseyNumber], [a1].[MarketValue], [a1].[PlayerCard], [a1].[Position], [a1].[StartDate], [a1].[SportsMember_DivisionId]

    WHERE [a1].[UserType] IN (N'UserBaseModel', N'ClubAdministrator', N'ClubManager', N'DivisionManager', N'Fan', N'Officials', N'Player', N'SportsMember', N'SystemAdministrator')

ORDER BY [t].[StartDate] DESC
